It will introduce your child to the world of multiplication using 3D animated dragons that guide them through 12 different environments, including a lagoon, a Halloween inspired level, a mountain, caves, a winter setting, and more! It has been used for generations, and proven its success over and over again. Our second memory device, the memory palace, is one of the oldest and most successful tools in the book! This method goes back to the ancient Greeks, and involves imagining a familiar environment (like your home) and associating the things to be remembered with particular areas or aspects of that environment.  The visual and spatial qualities of this form provide additional contact points that aid in the creation of cognitive associations with the thing that we want to remember. This creates more access routes for our brains to get at the desired information, and thus increases ease of recall. Nachdem Ihr Kind ein paar Mal freundliche Mathematik benutzt, beginnt die App, Fragen zu beantworten, die die Fähigkeit deines Kindes vorsichtig herausfordern, ohne den Fortschritt zu verhindern. Das Ziel ist es, diese süße Stelle zu erreichen, wo Fragen nicht zu einfach und nicht allzu schwierig sind, um maximale Vorteile zu erzielen.\r\n \r\nMeine Motivation für die Entwicklung von Friendly Mathematik wuchs aus der Beobachtung meiner beiden Kinder interagieren mit verschiedenen Mathe-Anwendungen im Laufe der Jahre. Ich bemerkte, dass einige Apps zu hart auf die Kinder waren, mit negativen Scoring, die in eine Menge Tränen und Frustration führte. Andere Apps waren zeitgesteuerte Spiele mit mehrfachen Auswahl Antworten. Meine Sorge mit denen war, dass Kinder gelernt, schnell drücken Sie die richtigen Tasten ohne viel Verständnis für das Thema.\r\n\r\nFreundliche Mathematik wurde entwickelt, um einige dieser Bedenken zu lösen. Mit freundlichen Mathematik, Kinder sind nicht zeitgesteuert, um ihnen Zeit zu erlauben, zu denken, Wissen zu konsolidieren und wirklich Probleme zu verstehen. Falsche Antworten werden nicht bestraft und die App bietet oft zwei Chancen. Ich glaube, dass dieser Ansatz den Geist des Lernens und Experimentierens fördert. Positive Verstärkung wird verwendet, nicht negativ bewertet. Dies verhindert, dass Kinder negative Haltungen gegenüber Mathematik bilden und ihr Selbstwertgefühl schützen. Das einfache visuelle Design der Apps hilft Kindern, sich auf Maths mit minimalen Ablenkungen zu konzentrieren, so dass Lernen leicht in Schulprüfungen und Real Life Szenarien übertragen werden kann.\r\n \r\nFreundliche Mathematik versorgt Ihr Kind mit Belohnungen in Form von Sammlerleistungen. Für die beste Wirkung werden die Eltern ermutigt, zusätzliche positive Verstärkung durch die Verknüpfung von App-Leistungen mit zusätzlichen Belohnungen zu bieten. Sie wissen am besten, was für Ihr Kind funktioniert, ob es sich um ein zusätzliches Taschengeld, Bildschirmzeit, die sie auf eine Reise oder gar nichts bringt. Jede Leistung wird durch die Beantwortung von 100 Fragen korrekt freigegeben, was in einer Sitzung oder zwei durchgeführt werden kann. Zu wenig Gebrauch kann nicht optimale Vorteile bieten, aber zu viel Gebrauch kann zu negativen Einstellungen und Müdigkeit führen. Wieder wissen Sie am besten, was für Ihr Kind optimal ist.\r\n \r\nFreundliche Mathematik kann von bis zu fünf Kindern verwendet werden, sofern sie einen Computer teilen. The game is played with a standard deck of cards (including 2 jokers). \r\n\r\nPlayers are dealt a total of 12 cards.  The remaining 6 cards are dealt face down into the 'Kitty'.  Each player will bid starting clockwise from the dealer (dealer bids last).  \r\nThe bid consists of a bid number and description.  The bid number is the number of tricks (books) a player believes his partnership can achieve over 6. For example, a bid of 4 = 10 books. \r\n\r\nThe bid description indicates a bid direction (High or Low) or whether the bid is a 'No' trump. A bid direction of High (Uptown) indicates A,K,Q... are the highest value cards. A bid direction of Low (Downtown, Special) indicates A,2,3... are the highest value cards. A 'No' trump bid indicates that each suit has equal weight and the lead card can not be 'cut'.  The bid direction of a 'No' bid is specified after winning the bid.\r\nBid numbers can range from 3 - 7.  The Option screen gives the player the option of playing with a minimum of 3 or 4.\r\nBid descriptions have the following weights:  'No' > 'Low' > 'High'.  The Option screen allows the player to play make 'Low' and 'High' equal in weight: 'No' > 'Low' = 'High'. \r\n\r\nThe highest bidder indicates a 'trump' suit or in the case of a 'No' bid indicates the direction (High/Low).  The jokers become the highest value cards in the indicated 'trump' suit.  For example, if Diamonds were called as 'trump' the highest value cards for a 'High' direction would be:  Big Joker, Little Joker, A, K,...  In the case of a 'No' bid, the Big Joker and Little Joker have no value and should be discarded as soon as possible.\r\n\r\nThe bid winner will start play as the lead player.  The remaining players must play a card in the same suit as the lead card if available. If the player does not have a card in that suit they may play another suit. The highest value card in the lead suit wins the sequence unless a trump card is played in which case the highest trump card wins the sequence. The winner of the sequence will be the lead player in the following sequence. \r\n\r\nGame Options\r\n\r\nPractice Mode:  The computer will not bid.  Allowing the player to always win bid and practice different plays.\r\nScoring - Conventional and Progressive:  With Conventional scoring the bid winner may go into negatives if the bid is not acheived. :\r\nThe Fall of the Dungeon Guardians is an RPG Dungeon Crawler game, in First Person View, inspired by classics like Dungeon Master™ and Might & Magic®, but featuring a modern combat system based on the triptych “tank/damage dealer/healer” mechanism.\r\n\r\nStory :\r\nYou’re a newly employed guard of a prison deep inside a dungeon. The night of your arrival, strange things happen and when you wake up in the morning, all prisoners have escaped amidst chaos. The warden wisely decides to leave the dungeon as quickly as possible, while tasking you to run after the escaping prisoners. You then assemble your team and venture into the mysterious dungeon.\r\n\r\nA Call For Adventure :\r\nEnter a big, massive dungeon, full of danger, mystery and secrets.\r\nFight your way through hordes of enemies and powerful creatures.\r\nExplore intricate corridors, underground palaces, mines fallen into oblivion and evil crypts.\r\nSolve puzzles, avoid deadly traps, uncover hidden passages, and keep your bearing through mazes & hallways.\r\n\r\nCharacter Building :\r\nYou’ll take command of a party of 4 guardians. Each guardian comes with a set of spells & abilities, with new ones appearing over the course of the adventure.\r\nFor each new level reached, the guardians get a point to use in their talent trees, allowing them to reinforce their abilities or gain new powers.\r\nThere are 4 classes to choose from: the warrior, the healer, the mage & the rogue. Each class has 3 specializations represented by a talent tree, and each specialization comes with its own set of abilities. So you have 12 base build-ups. In addition, your guardians can choose freely to spend their talent points in any of the 3 specializations of their class, allowing for even more varied set-ups.\r\n\r\nThe dungeon is filled with loot: epic armors, legendary weapons and mystical, magical items. Often when you kill a group of enemies, they’ll drop a random piece of equipment that one of your guardians can use, raising more and more of their powers.\r\n\r\nEvolved Combat System :\r\nThe combat is focused on the triptych “tank/damage dealer/healer” mechanism, coupled with an exciting threat mechanism: your healer’s spells directly threaten all the enemies nearby, and thus your tank must use his abilities to attract their wrath and protect the healer. The tank must then be able to mitigate a lot of the enemy damage using his defensive skills.\r\nYour last 2 guardians will be the damage dealers, trying to kill the enemies as fast as possible, while they’re busy with the tank.\r\nAll guardians get a lot of abilities and not only will using the right one at the right moment be essential to your party’s survival, but also combining different abilities in sequence to maximize their efficiency will be required to vanquish your strongest foes.\r\nIt sounds like a lot, but fortunately the game comes with an active pause: you can pause the game whenever you feel like it, check everything, queue the next abilities for your guardians, and then resume the game.\r\n\r\nYou don’t like tanks, or you don’t like pausing the game? No problem, just lower the game difficulty, and you’ll be able to play without a real tank or pausing. You can precisely tune the difficulty at any time during your exploration.\r\n\r\nUnlike old-school FPV Dungeon Crawlers, you don’t have to strafe-turn-strafe-turn all the time in Dungeon Guardians. Your tank comes with serious defensive skills (armor, dodge & parry) that let him handle most of the enemy attacks, as long as the healer backs him up. So most fights are done while standing your ground.\r\nHowever, occasionally your whole party will have to dodge some extremely powerful enemy attacks, usually by walking back, so you’ll still need some moving reflexes and awareness of your surroundings during the fights.\r\n\r\nBuilt-in Map editor & Modding :\r\nThe game comes with a full featured map editor, letting you create your own dungeons. The basics are very simple, but a bit of learning will be required to handle the more advanced puzzle mechanisms.\r\nAdditionally, with the Modding SDK, you’ll be able to fine-tune the existing enemies, classes, specializations, abilities, talents, gear, and enchantments, and with a bit of dedication you should be able to add your own, and even add sound FX or music.\r\n\r\nGame Features :\r\n    - 4-character Party\r\n    - Grid-based movement : your party moves 1 square at the time, and turns by a quarter\r\n    - First person view\r\n    - 4 classes, 12 specializations\r\n    - 5 playable races : human, dwarf, elf, dark elf, halfling\r\n    - Active pause (ie: you can pause the game and still queue commands for your party members), and numerous optional auto-pauses\r\n    - 25-50 hours of gameplay, depending on your own skills and the difficulty settings\r\n    - 20 bosses\r\n    - 100 kinds of creatures (including variations)\r\n    - Puzzles (the few ones required to finish the game are easy to solve)\r\n    - A lot of tactical combat\r\n    - Built-in Map Editor & Modding support \r\n\r\nReviews :\r\n“The combat is exquisitely balanced. Yes, it relies on the generic trio of a tank to absorb enemy attacks, a healer to keep the tank standing, and two damage-dealers to take out the actual enemies. Yes, that’s a bit of an unexpected approach for a game that’s so old school in every other aspect. But it works so shockingly well, it’ll give you a brand new appreciation to the entire mechanic.”\r\n4/5 – IndieGameReviewer http://indiegamereviewer.com/review-the-fall-of-the-dungeon-guardians/\r\n\r\n“By addressing most of the shortcomings found in old school 3D dungeon crawlers, Mana Games has created an addictive adventure game worth exploring.”\r\nB+ – Defunct Games http://www.defunctgames.com/courant/951/the-fall-of-the-dungeon-guardians\r\n\r\nLet's Play :\r\n“The Fall Of The Dungeon Guardians is a fantastic take on the First Person Dungeon Crawlers of old.
